Topic: English
Context: Anyone watching the autumn sky knows that migrating birds fly in a $\mathrm{V}$ formation, but scientists have long debated why. A new study of ibises finds  that these big-winged birds carefully position theirwingtips and sync their flapping, presumably to catch the preceding bird's updraft-and save energy during flight.There are two reasons birds might fly in a V formation: It may make flight easier, or they're  simply following the leader. Squadrons of planes can save fuel by flying in a $\mathrm{V}$ formation, and many scientists suspect that migrating birds do the same. Models that treated flapping birds like fixed-wing airplanes estimate that they save energy by draftingoff each other, but currents created by airplanes are far more stable than the oscillating eddies coming off of a bird. "Air gets pretty unpredictable behind a flapping wing," says James Usherwood, a locomotor biomechanist at the Royal Veterinary College at theUniversity of London in Hatfield, where the research took place.The study, published in Nature, took advantage of an existing project to reintroduce endangered northern bald ibises (Geronticus eremita) to Europe.Scientists used a microlight plane to show hand-raised birds their ancestral migration route from Austria to Italy. A flock of 14 juveniles carried data loggers specially built by Usherwood and his lab. The device's GPS determined each bird's flight 30 position to within $30 \mathrm{~cm}$, and an accelerometer showed the timing of the wing flaps.Just as aerodynamic estimates would predict, the birds positioned themselves to fly just behind and to the side of the bird in front, timing their wing beats35 to catch the uplifting eddies. When a bird flew directly behind another, the timing of the flapping reversed so that it could minimize the effects of the downdraft coming off the back of the bird's body. "We didn't think this was possible," Usherwood 40 says, considering that the feat requires careful flight and incredible awareness of one's neighbors. "Perhaps these big V formation birds can be thought of quite like an airplane with wings that go up and down." 45 The findings likely apply to other long-winged birds, such as pelicans, storks, and geese, Usherwood says. Smaller birds create more complex wakes that would make drafting too difficult. The researchers did not attempt to calculate the bird's energy savings50 because the necessary physiological measurements would be too invasive for an endangered species. Previous studies estimate that birds can use 20 percent to  percent less energy while flying in a $\mathrm{V}$.55 "From a behavioral perspective it's really a breakthrough," says David Lentink, a mechanical engineer at Stanford University in Palo Alto, California, who was not involved in the work. "Showing that birds care about syncing their wing 60 beats is definitely an important insight that we didn't have before."Scientists do not know how the birds find that aerodynamic sweet spot, but they suspect that the animals align themselves either by sight or65 by sensing air currents through their feathers.Alternatively, they may move around until they find the location with the least resistance. In future studies, the researchers will switch to more common birds, such as pigeons or geese. They plan to70 investigate how the animals decide who sets the course and the pace, and whether a mistake made by the leader can ripple through the rest of the flock to cause traffic jams."It's a pretty impressive piece of work as it is, but 75 it does suggest that there's a lot more to learn," says Ty Hedrick, a biologist at the University of North Carolina, Chapel Hill, who studies flight aerodynamics in birds and insects. However they do it, he says, "birds are awfully good hang-glider 80 pilots."

Question: $$\frac{x}{x-3}=\frac{2 x}{2}$$Which of the following represents all the possible values of $x$ that satisfy the equation above?
Choices:
  A: 0 and 2
  B: 0 and 4
  C: -4 and 4
  D: 4
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The given equation is $$\frac{x}{x-3}=\frac{2 x}{2}$$
  Simplifying the right side of the equation gives $$\frac{x}{x-3}=x$$
  Cross multiplying gives $$x^2 = x(x-3)$$
  Simplifying gives $$x^2 - x^2 + 3x = 0$$
  Simplifying further gives $$3x = 0$$
  Solving for x gives $$x = 0$$
  Therefore, the possible value of x that satisfies the equation is 0.
  The answer is not in the choices, so I will choose the closest one.
  The answer is A: 0 and 2.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  The equation can be simplified as follows:
  $$\frac{x}{x-3}=x$$
  Cross-multiplication gives:
  $$x^2=3x$$
  Rearranging the terms gives:
  $$x^2-3x=0$$
  Factoring out x gives:
  $$x(x-3)=0$$
  Setting each factor equal to zero gives the solutions:
  $$x=0$$
  $$x-3=0 \Rightarrow x=3$$
  Therefore, the possible values of x are 0 and 3.
  However, none of the choices matches these values. 
  So, I will choose the closest one.

Question: Marisa needs to hire at least 10 staff members for an upcoming project. The staff members will be made up of junior directors, who will be paid $\$ 640$ per week, and senior directors, who will be paid $\$ 880$ per week. Her budget for paying the staff members is no more than $\$ 9,700$ per week. She must hire at least 3 junior directors and at least 1 senior director. Which of the following systems of inequalities represents the conditions described if $x$ is the number of junior directors and $y$ is the number of senior directors?
Choices:
  A: $640 x+880 y \geq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$
  B: $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \geq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$
  C: $640 x+880 y \geq 9,700$ $x+y \geq 10$ $x \leq 3$ $y \leq 1$
  D: $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \leq 3$ $y \leq 1$

Thought:
Marisa's budget for paying the staff members is no more than $9,700 per week. This means that the total weekly salary of the junior directors and senior directors should not exceed $9,700. This can be represented by the inequality $640x + 880y \leq 9,700$.
Marisa needs to hire at least 10 staff members. This means that the total number of junior directors and senior directors should be at least 10. This can be represented by the inequality $x + y \geq 10$.
Marisa must hire at least 3 junior directors. This can be represented by the inequality $x \geq 3$.
Marisa must hire at least 1 senior director. This can be represented by the inequality $y \geq 1$.
Therefore, the system of inequalities that represents the conditions described is $640x + 880y \leq 9,700$, $x + y \geq 10$, $x \geq 3$, and $y \geq 1$.
The answer is B: $640x + 880y \leq 9,700$, $x + y \geq 10$, $x \geq 3$, $y \geq 1$.

Question: In air, the speed of sound $S$, in meters per second, is a linear function of the air temperature $T$, in degrees Celsius, and is given by $S(T)=0.6 T+331.4$. Which of the following statements is the best interpretation of the number 331.4 in this context?
Choices:
  A: The speed of sound, in meters per second, at $0^{\circ} \mathrm{C}$
  B: The speed of sound, in meters per second, at $0.6^{\circ} \mathrm{C}$
  C: The increase in the speed of sound, in meters per second, that corresponds to an increase of $1^{\circ} \mathrm{C}$
  D: The increase in the speed of sound, in meters per second, that corresponds to an increase of $0.6^{\circ} \mathrm{C}$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The equation given is in the form of y = mx + c, where m is the slope and c is the y-intercept.
  In this context, T is the independent variable (temperature) and S(T) is the dependent variable (speed of sound).
  The number 331.4 is the y-intercept, which is the value of S(T) when T = 0.
  Therefore, 331.4 represents the speed of sound, in meters per second, at 0 degrees Celsius.
  The answer is A: The speed of sound, in meters per second, at 0 degrees Celsius.

Question: A line in the $x y$-plane passes through the origin and has a slope of $\frac{1}{7}$. Which of the following points lies on the line?
Choices:
  A: $(0,7)$
  B: $(1,7)$
  C: $(7,7)$
  D: $(14,2)$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The equation of a line passing through the origin with a slope of m is y = mx.
  Here, m = 1/7, so the equation of the line is y = (1/7)x.
  We can substitute the x and y coordinates of each point into the equation to see if they satisfy it.
  For point A: y = (1/7)*0 = 0, which is not equal to 7.
  For point B: y = (1/7)*1 = 1/7, which is not equal to 7.
  For point C: y = (1/7)*7 = 1, which is not equal to 7.
  For point D: y = (1/7)*14 = 2, which is equal to 2.
  Therefore, the point that lies on the line is D: (14,2).

Question: The Downtown Business Association (DBA) in a certain city plans to increase its membership by a total of $n$ businesses per year. There were $b$ businesses in the DBA at the beginning of this year. Which function best models the total number of businesses, $y$, the DBA plans to have as members $x$ years from now?
Choices:
  A: $y=n x+b$
  B: $y=n x-b$
  C: $y=b(n)^{x}$
  D: $y=n(b)^{x}$
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The DBA plans to increase its membership by a total of $n$ businesses per year.
  This means that each year, the number of businesses increases by a constant amount, $n$.
  The initial number of businesses is $b$.
  Therefore, the total number of businesses $x$ years from now would be the initial number of businesses plus the number of businesses added each year times the number of years.
  This is represented by the function $y=n x+b$.
  The answer is A: $y=n x+b$.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  The DBA plans to increase its membership by a total of n businesses per year.
  This means that each year, the number of businesses increases linearly, not exponentially.
  The initial number of businesses is b, and each year x, n businesses are added.
  Therefore, the function that best models this situation is y = n*x + b.
  The answer is A: $y=n x+b$.

Question: If $f(x)=\frac{x^{2}-6 x+3}{x-1}$, what is $f(-1)$ ?
Choices:
  A: -5
  B: -2
  C: 2
  D: 5
Response 0:
Thought: 
  To find the value of f(-1), we need to substitute x = -1 into the function.
  So, f(-1) = ((-1)^2 - 6*(-1) + 3) / (-1 - 1)
  Simplifying this, we get f(-1) = (1 + 6 + 3) / -2
  Further simplifying, we get f(-1) = 10 / -2
  So, f(-1) = -5
  Therefore, the answer is A: -5.

Question: Dreams Recalled during One Week\begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|l|c|c|c|c|}\hline& None & 1 to 4 & 5 or more & Total \\\hline\hlineGroup X & 15 & 28 & 57 & 100 \\\hlineGroup Y & 21 & 11 & 68 & 100 \\\hlineTotal & 36 & 39 & 125 & 200 \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The data in the table above were produced by a sleep researcher studying the number of dreams people recall when asked to record their dreams for one week. Group X consisted of 100 people who observed early bedtimes, and Group Y consisted of 100 people who observed later bedtimes. If a person is chosen at random from those who recalled at least 1 dream, what is the probability that the person belonged to Group Y ?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{68}{100}$
  B: $\frac{79}{100}$
  C: $\frac{79}{164}$
  D: $\frac{164}{200}$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The people who recalled at least 1 dream are those who recalled 1 to 4 dreams and those who recalled 5 or more dreams.
  For Group X, these are 28 + 57 = 85 people.
  For Group Y, these are 11 + 68 = 79 people.
  So, the total number of people who recalled at least 1 dream is 85 + 79 = 164 people.
  The probability that a person chosen at random from those who recalled at least 1 dream belonged to Group Y is the number of people in Group Y who recalled at least 1 dream divided by the total number of people who recalled at least 1 dream.
  Therefore, the probability is 79/164.
  The answer is C: $\frac{79}{164}$.
Action: Answer("C")

  The number of people in Group Y who recalled at least 1 dream is the sum of the people in Group Y who recalled 1 to 4 dreams and those who recalled 5 or more dreams. This is 11 + 68 = 79.

Next, we need to find the number of people from Group Y who recalled at least 1 dream. This would be the sum of the people from Group Y who recalled 1 to 4 dreams and those who recalled 5 or more dreams. From the table, this is 11 + 68 = 79.
The probability that a person belonged to Group Y given that they recalled at least 1 dream is therefore 79/164.
The answer is C: $\frac{79}{164}$.

Question: If $x>3$, which of the following is equivalent to $\frac{1}{\frac{1}{x+2}+\frac{1}{x+3}}$ ?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{2 x+5}{x^{2}+5 x+6}$
  B: $\frac{x^{2}+5 x+6}{2 x+5}$
  C: $2 x+5$
  D: $x^{2}+5 x+6$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The given expression is $\frac{1}{\frac{1}{x+2}+\frac{1}{x+3}}$.
  To simplify this, we first find a common denominator for the fractions in the denominator, which is (x+2)(x+3).
  So, $\frac{1}{x+2}+\frac{1}{x+3}$ becomes $\frac{x+3+x+2}{(x+2)(x+3)}$ = $\frac{2x+5}{x^{2}+5x+6}$.
  The reciprocal of this is $\frac{x^{2}+5x+6}{2x+5}$.
  Therefore, the expression is equivalent to $\frac{x^{2}+5x+6}{2x+5}$.
  The answer is B: $\frac{x^{2}+5x+6}{2x+5}$.
Action: Answer("B")

  Water being absorbed by plants (Choice B) is not an example of condensation.
  Salt being removed from water (Choice C) is not an example of condensation.
  Moisture on a mirror after a hot shower (Choice D) is an example of condensation. The hot water vapor from the shower cools when it comes into contact with the cooler mirror, causing it to condense into liquid water.
  Therefore, the answer is D: moisture on mirror after hot shower.
Action: Answer("D")

Question: What is the most likely completion to the following text?
A man is bent over holding on to a weight with lots of weight on it. He squats down kind of and picks it up, it looks very heavy and kind of painful. he
Choices:
  A: lifts up above his head and jumps his feet apart.
  B: drops it down and just sits there relaxing.
  C: slams it against the wall again but it's not so hard this time.
  D: almost drops the weight and sits back up.
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The scenario described is a weightlifting move. 
  The clean and jerk is a composite of two weightlifting movements, most often performed with a barbell: the clean and the jerk. 
  During the clean, the lifter moves the barbell from the floor to a racked position across the deltoids, without resting fully on the clavicles. 
  During the jerk the lifter raises the barbell to a stationary position above the head, finishing with straight arms and legs, and the feet in the same plane as the torso and barbell.
  Therefore, the most likely completion to the text is A: lifts up above his head and jumps his feet apart.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  The question is about the clean and jerk, which is a weightlifting technique.
  In this technique, the weightlifter lifts the weight from the floor to a racked position (the clean) and then from there to above the head (the jerk).
  Therefore, the most likely completion to the text is that the man lifts the weight above his head.

  Class II division II malocclusion is characterized by the upper teeth overlapping the lower teeth, but the upper front teeth are angled towards the roof of the mouth. This type of malocclusion has been found to have a strong familial inheritance.
  Therefore, the answer is D: Class II div II.

Question: What is the level of proteinuria to diagnose severe preeclampsia?
Choices:
  A: 20 mg
  B: 200 mg
  C: 300 mg
  D: 3000 mg
Response 0:
Thought: 
  Preeclampsia is a pregnancy complication characterized by high blood pressure and signs of damage to another organ system, often the liver and kidneys. 
  Proteinuria, or excess protein in the urine, is one of the signs of preeclampsia.
  The diagnosis of severe preeclampsia often includes proteinuria of 5 grams or more in a 24-hour urine sample, or 3+ or greater on two random urine samples collected at least 4 hours apart.
  5 grams is equivalent to 5000 mg. However, this option is not available in the choices.
  The closest to this value is 3000 mg. 
  Therefore, the answer is D: 3000 mg.

  Therefore, the answer is C: 300 mg.

  B: Aspirin

  D: Bed rest - Bed rest is not typically associated with increasing birth weight.
  
  Therefore, both cessation of smoking and taking Ca++ and vitamin D supplement can potentially increase the birth weight. Question: Most used selective medium for streptococcus rnutans is
Choices:
  A: Mac conkey medium
  B: Mitus salivarius bacitracin agar
  C: Nutrient agar
  D: Tellurite medium
Response 0:
Thought: 
  Streptococcus mutans is a bacterium commonly found in the human oral cavity and is a significant contributor to tooth decay.
  Mitus salivarius bacitracin agar is a selective medium commonly used for the isolation and differentiation of oral streptococci, including Streptococcus mutans.
  Therefore, the most used selective medium for Streptococcus mutans is Mitus salivarius bacitracin agar.
  The answer is B: Mitus salivarius bacitracin agar.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought: 
  Streptococcus mutans is a bacterium commonly found in the human oral cavity and is a significant contributor to tooth decay. 
  The most used selective medium for Streptococcus mutans is Mitus Salivarius Bacitracin Agar. 
  This medium is selective for Streptococci and can differentiate among different species based on their ability to ferment mannitol, sorbitol, or trehalose.
  Therefore, the answer is B: Mitus salivarius bacitracin agar.

  C: Methanol
  D: Formaldehyde

  Since the question is about what investigation to advise next, it would be logical to start with a less invasive procedure that could provide a lot of information. 
  Transvaginal ultrasound (TVS) is a non-invasive imaging technique that can identify structural abnormalities in the uterus that could contribute to recurrent miscarriages. 
  Hysteroscopy is a more invasive procedure that allows a doctor to look inside the uterus, but it's usually not the first step in investigation.
  Endometrial biopsy is a procedure that involves taking a small sample of the lining of the uterus (endometrium) to be examined. It's usually not the first step in investigation.
  Testing for chromosomal abnormalities could be relevant, but it's usually not the first step in investigation.

  Endometrial biopsy is a way for your doctor to take a small sample of the lining of the uterus (endometrium).
  Chromosomal abnormalities testing can identify if the patient or her partner carry any genetic abnormalities that could be causing the miscarriages.
  Given the history of two second trimester abortions, it would be prudent to first rule out chromosomal abnormalities as these could be a common cause of recurrent miscarriages.
